(\n\t\"context\"\n\t\"encoding/base64\"\n\t\"testing\"\n\t\"time\"\n\n\t\"github.com/jonboulle/clockwork\"\n\t\"github.com/stretchr/testify/require\"\n\n\t\"github.com/gravitational/teleport\"\n\t\"github.com/gravitational/teleport/api/types\"\n\t\"github.com/gravitational/teleport/lib/auth\"\n\t\"github.com/gravitational/teleport/lib/auth/mocku2f\"\n\t\"github.com/gravitational/teleport/lib/auth/u2f\"\n\t\"github.com/gravitational/teleport/lib/services\"\n)\n\n// TestRegression demonstrates the multi-device U2F authentication bug.\n// When a user registers multiple U2F tokens, only the first token is issued\n// a challenge during login, preventing use of other registered devices.\nfunc TestRegression(t *testing.T) {\n\tctx := context.Background()\n\tclock := clockwork.NewFakeClock()\n\n\t// Create test auth server with U2F enabled\n\tas, err := auth.NewTestAuthServer(auth.TestAuthServerConfig{\n\t\tDir:   t.TempDir(),\n\t\tClock: clock,\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\tdefer as.Close()\n\n\t// Set up U2F configuration\n\tauthPref, err := services.NewAuthPreference(types.AuthPreferenceSpecV2{\n\t\tType: teleport.Local,\n\t\tU2F: &types.U2F{\n\t\t\tAppID:  \"teleport\",\n\t\t\tFacets: []string{\"teleport\"},\n\t\t},\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\terr = as.AuthServer.SetAuthPreference(authPref)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\t// Create test user\n\tuser, _, err := as.AuthServer.Identity\n\n\t// Create in-memory storage for U2F challenges\n\tu2fStorage, err := u2f.InMemoryAuthenticationStorage(identityBackend)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\t// Register first U2F device\n\tu2fDev1, err := mocku2f.Create()\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\t// Perform first registration\n\tregChallenge1, err := u2f.NewChallenge(u2fPref.AppID, u2fPref.Facets)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\tregResp1, err := u2fDev1.RegisterResponse(&u2f.RegisterChallenge{\n\t\tChallenge: regChallenge1.Challenge,\n\t\tAppID:     regChallenge1.AppID,\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\tmfaDev1, err := u2f.NewDevice(\"u2f-device-1\", &u2f.Registration{\n\t\tKeyHandle: u2fDev1.KeyHandle,\n\t\tPubKey:    u2fDev1.PrivateKey.PublicKey,\n\t}, clock.Now())\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\t// Store first device\n\terr = identityBackend.UpsertMFADevice(ctx, username, mfaDev1)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\t// Register second U2F device\n\tu2fDev2, err := mocku2f.Create()\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\tregChallenge2, err := u2f.NewChallenge(u2fPref.AppID, u2fPref.Facets)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\tregResp2, err := u2fDev2.RegisterResponse(&u2f.RegisterChallenge{\n\t\tChallenge: regChallenge2.Challenge,\n\t\tAppID:     regChallenge2.AppID,\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\tmfaDev2, username)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\tu2fDevices := make([]*types.MFADevice, 0)\n\tfor _, dev := range devs {\n\t\tif dev.GetU2F() != nil {\n\t\t\tu2fDevices = append(u2fDevices, dev)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\trequire.Len(t, u2fDevices, 2, \"Expected 2 U2F devices to be registered\")\n\n\t// TEST 1: Old API (CheckU2FSignChallenge) - only returns challenge for FIRST device\n\t// This demonstrates the bug: only one challenge is returned even though user has 2 devices\n\tchallenge1, err := as.AuthServer.CheckU2FSignChallenge(ctx, username)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\trequire.NotNil(t, challenge1)\n\n\t// The challenge should be for only one device (the bug!)\n\t// Extract which device this challenge is for\n\tif challenge1 == nil {\n\t\tt.Fatal(\"Challenge should not be nil\")\n\t}\n\n\tchallenge1KeyHandle := challenge1.KeyHandle\n\tchallenge1Matches := false\n\tfor _, dev := range u2fDevices {\n\t\tu2fDev := dev.GetU2F()\n\t\tkh := base64.URLEncoding.WithPadding(base64.NoPadding).EncodeToString(u2fDev.KeyHandle)\n\t\tif kh == challenge1KeyHandle {\n\t\t\tchallenge1Matches = true\n\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\trequire.True(t, challenge1Matches, \"Challenge should match one of the registered devices\")\n\n\t// TEST 2: New API (CreateAuthenticateChallenge) - correctly returns challenges for ALL devices\n\t// This is the fixed implementation that properly supports multi-device U2F\n\tchallenge2, err := as.AuthServer.CreateAuthenticateChallenge(ctx, username, false)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\trequire.NotNil(t, challenge2)\n\n\t// The challenge should have U2F challenges for BOTH devices (this is the correct behavior)\n\trequire.NotEmpty(t, challenge2.U2F, \"Challenge should contain U2F challenges\")\n\n\t// This test demonstrates the regression: we expect the number of U2F challenges\n\t// to match the number of registered U2F devices\n\texpectedDeviceCount := 2\n\tactualChallengeCount := len(challenge2.U2F)\n\n\tif actualChallengeCount != expectedDeviceCount {\n\t\tt.Logf(\"REGRESSION BUG DETECTED:\")\n\t\tt.Logf(\"Expected %d U2F challenges for %d registered devices\", expectedDeviceCount, expectedDeviceCount)\n\t\tt.Logf(\"Got %d U2F challenges\", actualChallengeCount)\n\t\tt.Logf(\"This means only %d/%d registered U2F devices can be used during authentication\", actualChallengeCount, expectedDeviceCount)\n\n\t\t// This should fail on buggy code and pass on fixed code\n\t\tt.Errorf(\"Multi-device U2F authentication regression: expected %d challenges, got %d\", expectedDeviceCount, actualChallengeCount)\n\t}\n\n\t// Verify that the challenges are for different devices (not duplicates)\n\tchallengeKeyHandles := make(map[string]bool)\n\tfor _, ch := range challenge2.U2F {\n\t\tchallengeKeyHandles[ch.KeyHandle] = true\n\t}\n\trequire.Len(t, challengeKeyHandles, expectedDeviceCount, \"All U2F challenges should be for different devices\")\n\n\t// Verify all registered devices have challenges\n\tfor _, dev := range u2fDevices {\n\t\tu2fDev := dev.GetU2F()\n\t\tdeviceKeyHandle := base64.URLEncoding.WithPadding(base64.NoPadding).EncodeToString(u2fDev.KeyHandle)\n\t\trequire.True(t, challengeKeyHandles[deviceKeyHandle], \"Every registered U2F device should have a challenge\")\n\t}\n\n\t// TEST 3: Demonstrate client/server compatibility issue\n\t// When client sends response for device 2, but server only issued challenge for device 1\n\tauthChallenge1, err := u2f.AuthenticateInit(ctx, u2f.AuthenticateInitParams{\n\t\tAppConfig:  *u2fPref,\n\t\tDev:        mfaDev1,\n\t\tStorageKey: username,\n\t\tStorage:    u2fStorage,\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, authChallenge1.KeyHandle,\n\t\tAppID:     authChallenge1.AppID,\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\t// This should work - device 1 authentication succeeds\n\terr = u2f.AuthenticateVerify(ctx, u2f.AuthenticateVerifyParams{\n\t\tDev:        mfaDev1,\n\t\tResp:       authResp1,\n\t\tStorageKey: username,\n\t\tStorage:    u2fStorage,\n\t\tClock:      clock,\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err, \"Device 1 authentication should succeed\")\n\n\t// Now try with device 2 - this demonstrates the problem\n\t// If the client only received a challenge for device 1, it cannot use device u2fStorage,\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\tauthResp2, err := u2fDev2.SignResponse(&u2f.AuthenticateChallenge{\n\t\tChallenge: authChallenge2.Challenge,\n\t\tKeyHandle: actualChallengeCount, expectedDeviceCount)\n\n\t\t// This should fail on buggy code and pass on fixed code\n\t\tt.Errorf(\"Multi-device U2F authentication regression: expected %d challenges, got %d\", expectedDeviceCount, actualChallengeCount)\n\t}\n\n\t// Verify that the challenges are for different devices (not duplicates)\n\tchallengeKeyHandles := make(map[string]bool)\n\tfor _, ch := range u2fStorage,\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\tauthResp2, err := u2fDev2.SignResponse(&u2f.AuthenticateChallenge{\n\t\tChallenge: authChallenge2.Challenge,\n\t\tKeyHandle: TestRegression demonstrates the multi-device U2F authentication bug.\n// When a user registers multiple U2F tokens, the authentication challenge\n// generation may not include all devices, limiting which hardware tokens\n// can be used during login.\nfunc TestRegression(t *testing.T) {\n\tctx := context.Background()\n\tclock := clockwork.NewFakeClock()\n\n\t// Create test auth server with U2F enabled\n\tas, err := auth.NewTestAuthServer(auth.TestAuthServerConfig{\n\t\tDir:   t.TempDir(),\n\t\tClock: clock,\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\t// Create a test TLS server for gRPC communication\n\tsrv, err := as.NewTestTLSServer()\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\t// Set up U2F configuration\n\tauthPref, err := services.NewAuthPreference(types.AuthPreferenceSpecV2{\n\t\tType: teleport.Local,\n\t\tU2F: &types.U2F{\n\t\t\tAppID:  \"teleport\",\n\t\t\tFacets: []string{\"teleport\"},\n\t\t},\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\terr = as.AuthServer.SetAuthPreference(authPref)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\t// Create test user\n\tuser, _, err := auth.CreateUserAndRole(as.AuthServer, \"testuser\", []string{\"role\"})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\tusername := user.GetName()\n\n\t// Create a gRPC client for the user\n\tcl, err := srv.NewClient(auth.TestUser(username))\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\t// Get U2F config from auth server\n\tu2fConfig, err := as.AuthServer.GetAuthPreference()\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\tu2fPref, err := u2fConfig.GetU2F()\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\t// ========== SETUP: Register First U2F Device ==========\n\tu2fDev1, err := mocku2f.Create()\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\tregChallenge1, err := u2f.NewChallenge(u2fPref.AppID, u2fPref.Facets)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\tregResp1, err := u2fDev1.RegisterResponse(&u2f.RegisterChallenge{\n\t\tChallenge: string(regChallenge1.Challenge),\n\t\tAppID:     regChallenge1.AppID,\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\t// Add first U2F device via gRPC stream\n\taddStream1, err := cl.AddMFADevice(ctx)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\terr = addStream1.Send(&proto.AddMFADeviceRequest{\n\t\tRequest: &proto.AddMFADeviceRequest_Init{\n\t\t\tInit: &proto.AddMFADeviceRequestInit{\n\t\t\t\tDeviceName: \"u2f-device-1\",\n\t\t\t\tType:       proto.AddMFADeviceRequestInit_U2F,\n\t\t\t},\n\t\t},\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\t// Receive auth challenge (should be empty for first device)\n\tauthChallenge1, err := addStream1.Recv()\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\texistingMFAChallenge1 := authChallenge1.GetExistingMFAChallenge()\n\trequire.NotNil(t, existingMFAChallenge1)\n\n\t// Send empty auth response since no existing devices\n\terr = addStream1.Send(&proto.AddMFADeviceRequest{\n\t\tRequest: &proto.AddMFADeviceRequest_ExistingMFAResponse{\n\t\t\tExistingMFAResponse: &proto.MFAAuthenticateResponse{},\n\t\t},\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\t// Receive register challenge\n\tregChallenge, err := addStream1.Recv()\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\tu2fRegChallenge := regChallenge.GetNewMFARegisterChallenge().GetU2F()\n\trequire.NotNil(t, u2fRegChallenge)\n\n\t// Send registration response\n\terr = addStream1.Send(&proto.AddMFADeviceRequest{\n\t\tRequest: &proto.AddMFADeviceRequest_NewMFARegisterResponse{\n\t\t\tNewMFARegisterResponse: &proto.MFARegisterResponse{\n\t\t\t\tResponse: &proto.MFARegisterResponse_U2F{\n\t\t\t\t\tU2F: &proto.U2FRegisterResponse{\n\t\t\t\t\t\tRegistrationData: regResp1.RegistrationData,\n\t\t\t\t\t\tClientData:       regResp1.ClientData,\n\t\t\t\t\t},\n\t\t\t\t},\n\t\t\t},\n\t\t},\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\t// Receive ack\n\tack1, err := addStream1.Recv()\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\trequire.NotNil(t, ack1.GetAck())\n\n\terr = addStream1.CloseSend()\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\t// ========== SETUP: Register Second U2F Device ==========\n\tu2fDev2, err := mocku2f.Create()\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\tregChallenge2, err := u2f.NewChallenge(u2fPref.AppID, u2fPref.Facets)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\tregResp2, err := u2fDev2.RegisterResponse(&u2f.RegisterChallenge{\n\t\tChallenge: string(regChallenge2.Challenge),\n\t\tAppID:     regChallenge2.AppID,\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\t// Add second U2F device via gRPC stream\n\taddStream2, err := cl.AddMFADevice(ctx)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\terr = addStream2.Send(&proto.AddMFADeviceRequest{\n\t\tRequest: &proto.AddMFADeviceRequest_Init{\n\t\t\tInit: &proto.AddMFADeviceRequestInit{\n\t\t\t\tDeviceName: \"u2f-device-2\",\n\t\t\t\tType:       proto.AddMFADeviceRequestInit_U2F,\n\t\t\t},\n\t\t},\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\t// Receive auth challenge (now should contain challenge for device 1)\n\tauthChallenge2, err := addStream2.Recv()\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\texistingMFAChallenge2 := authChallenge2.GetExistingMFAChallenge()\n\trequire.NotNil(t, existingMFAChallenge2)\n\n\t// THIS IS THE BUG: When adding a second U2F device,\n\t// existingMFAChallenge2.U2F should contain challenges for all existing U2F devices\n\t// In the buggy code, it will only contain ONE challenge even though we have 1 registered device\n\t// which is correct for this case, but demonstrates the structural issue.\n\n\t// Let's verify by checking the content\n\tu2fChallengesForSecondAdd := len(existingMFAChallenge2.U2F)\n\texpectedChallengesForSecondAdd := 1 // We've registered 1 device so far\n\n\tif u2fChallengesForSecondAdd != expectedChallengesForSecondAdd {\n\t\tt.Logf(\"WARNING: When adding second device, expected %d U2F challenges, got %d\",\n\t\t\texpectedChallengesForSecondAdd, u2fChallengesForSecondAdd)\n\t}\n\n\t// Send response using device 1\n\tif len(existingMFAChallenge2.U2F) > 0 {\n\t\tauthResp2, err := u2fDev1.SignResponse(&u2f.AuthenticateChallenge{\n\t\t\tChallenge: existingMFAChallenge2.U2F[0].Challenge,\n\t\t\tKeyHandle: existingMFAChallenge2.U2F[0].KeyHandle,\n\t\t\tAppID:     existingMFAChallenge2.U2F[0].AppID,\n\t\t})\n\t\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\t\terr = addStream2.Send(&proto.AddMFADeviceRequest{\n\t\t\tRequest: &proto.AddMFADeviceRequest_ExistingMFAResponse{\n\t\t\t\tExistingMFAResponse: &proto.MFAAuthenticateResponse{\n\t\t\t\t\tResponse: &proto.MFAAuthenticateResponse_U2F{\n\t\t\t\t\t\tU2F: &proto.U2FResponse{\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tKeyHandle:  authResp2.KeyHandle,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tClientData: authResp2.ClientData,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tSignature:  authResp2.SignatureData,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t},\n\t\t\t\t\t},\n\t\t\t\t},\n\t\t\t},\n\t\t})\n\t\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\t}\n\n\t// Receive register challenge for device 2\n\tregChallenge2Recv, err := addStream2.Recv()\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\tu2fRegChallenge2 := regChallenge2Recv.GetNewMFARegisterChallenge().GetU2F()\n\trequire.NotNil(t, u2fRegChallenge2)\n\n\t// Send registration response\n\terr = addStream2.Send(&proto.AddMFADeviceRequest{\n\t\tRequest: &proto.AddMFADeviceRequest_NewMFARegisterResponse{\n\t\t\tNewMFARegisterResponse: &proto.MFARegisterResponse{\n\t\t\t\tResponse: &proto.MFARegisterResponse_U2F{\n\t\t\t\t\tU2F: &proto.U2FRegisterResponse{\n\t\t\t\t\t\tRegistrationData: regResp2.RegistrationData,\n\t\t\t\t\t\tClientData:       regResp2.ClientData,\n\t\t\t\t\t},\n\t\t\t\t},\n\t\t\t},\n\t\t},\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\t// Receive ack\n\tack2, err := addStream2.Recv()\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\trequire.NotNil(t, ack2.GetAck())\n\n\terr = addStream2.CloseSend()\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\t// ========== REGRESSION TEST: Delete a Device with 2 U2F Devices Present ==========\n\t// Now we have 2 U2F devices registered.\n\t// When attempting to delete a device, the auth challenge should contain\n\t// challenges for ALL existing U2F devices.\n\n\t// Verify both devices are registered\n\tdevicesResp, err := cl.GetMFADevices(ctx, &proto.GetMFADevicesRequest{})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\tu2fDeviceCount := 0\n\tfor _, dev := range devicesResp.Devices {\n\t\tif dev.GetU2F() != nil {\n\t\t\tu2fDeviceCount++\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\trequire.Equal(t, 2, u2fDeviceCount, \"Expected 2 U2F devices to be registered\")\n\n\t// Attempt to delete one of the U2F devices\n\tdeleteStream, err := cl.DeleteMFADevice(ctx)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\terr = deleteStream.Send(&proto.DeleteMFADeviceRequest{\n\t\tRequest: &proto.DeleteMFADeviceRequest_Init{\n\t\t\tInit: &proto.DeleteMFADeviceRequestInit{\n\t\t\t\tDeviceName: \"u2f-device-1\",\n\t\t\t},\n\t\t},\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\t// Receive auth challenge\n\tdeleteAuthChallenge, err := deleteStream.Recv()\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\tdeleteChallenge := deleteAuthChallenge.GetMFAChallenge()\n\trequire.NotNil(t, deleteChallenge)\n\n\t// ========== REGRESSION BUG DETECTION ==========\n\t// This is the key regression test:\n\t// With 2 U2F devices registered, the authentication challenge should contain\n\t// challenges for BOTH devices so the user can choose which token to use.\n\t// In the buggy code, the challenge might only include 1 device.\n\n\tactualU2FChallengeCount := len(deleteChallenge.U2F)\n\texpectedU2FChallengeCount := 2 // We have 2 U2F devices\n\n\tif actualU2FChallengeCount != expectedU2FChallengeCount {\n\t\tt.Logf(\"REGRESSION BUG DETECTED:\")\n\t\tt.Logf(\"With %d U2F devices registered, the authentication challenge should contain %d U2F challenges\",\n\t\t\texpectedU2FChallengeCount, expectedU2FChallengeCount)\n\t\tt.Logf(\"Got %d U2F challenges instead\", actualU2FChallengeCount)\n\t\tt.Logf(\"This means only %d/%d registered U2F devices can be selected during authentication\",\n\t\t\tactualU2FChallengeCount, expectedU2FChallengeCount)\n\n\t\t// Fail if the number doesn't match\n\t\tt.Errorf(\"Multi-device U2F authentication regression: expected %d U2F challenges, got %d\",\n\t\t\texpectedU2FChallengeCount, actualU2FChallengeCount)\n\t}\n\n\t// Verify that the challenges are for different devices (not duplicates)\n\tchallengeKeyHandles := make(map[string]bool)\n\tfor _, ch := range deleteChallenge.U2F {\n\t\tchallengeKeyHandles[ch.KeyHandle] = true\n\t}\n\n\tif len(challengeKeyHandles) != expectedU2FChallengeCount {\n\t\tt.Errorf(\"Expected %d unique U2F challenges, got %d\",\n\t\t\texpectedU2FChallengeCount, len(challengeKeyHandles))\n\t}\n\n\t// Verify each registered device has a challenge\n\tdevicesResp2, err := cl.GetMFADevices(ctx, &proto.GetMFADevicesRequest{})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\tfor _, dev := range devicesResp2.Devices {\n\t\tu2fDev := dev.GetU2F()\n\t\tif u2fDev == nil {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\t\tdeviceKeyHandle := base64.URLEncoding.WithPadding(base64.NoPadding).EncodeToString(u2fDev.KeyHandle)\n\t\tif !challengeKeyHandles[deviceKeyHandle] {\n\t\t\tt.Errorf(\"U2F device %q should have a challenge but doesn't\", dev.GetName())\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Cleanup: Cancel the delete stream\n\tdeleteStream.CloseSend()\n\n\tt.Logf(\"Regression test completed successfully\")\n\tt.Logf(\"- Multiple U2F devices registered: PASS (%d devices)\", u2fDeviceCount)\n\tt.Logf(\"- Authentication challenge contains all device challenges: %v (%d/%d)\",\n\t\tactualU2FChallengeCount == expectedU2FChallengeCount, actualU2FChallengeCount, expectedU2FChallengeCount)\n}\n","structuredPatch":[{"oldStart":83,"oldLines":15,"newStart":83,"newLines":6,"lines":["   u2fDev1, err := mocku2f.Create()"," devicesResp.Devices {\n\t\tif dev.GetU2F() != nil {\n\t\t\tu2fDeviceCount++\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\trequire.Equal(t, 2, u2fDeviceCount, \"Expected 2 U2F devices to be registered\")\n\n\t// Attempt to delete one of the U2F devices\n\tdeleteStream, err := cl.DeleteMFADevice(ctx)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\terr = deleteStream.Send(&proto.DeleteMFADeviceRequest{\n\t\tRequest: &proto.DeleteMFADeviceRequest_Init{\n\t\t\tInit: &proto.DeleteMFADeviceRequestInit{\n\t\t\t\tDeviceName: \"u2f-device-1\",\n\t\t\t},\n\t\t},\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\t// Receive auth challenge\n\tdeleteAuthChallenge, err := deleteStream.Recv()\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\tdeleteChallenge := deleteAuthChallenge.GetMFAChallenge()\n\trequire.NotNil(t, deleteChallenge)\n\n\t// ========== REGRESSION BUG DETECTION ==========\n\t// This is the key regression test:\n\t// With 2 U2F devices registered, the authentication challenge should contain\n\t// challenges for BOTH devices so the user can choose which token to use.\n\t// In the buggy code, the challenge might only include 1 device.\n\n\tactualU2FChallengeCount := len(deleteChallenge.U2F)\n\texpectedU2FChallengeCount := 2 // We have 2 U2F devices\n\n\tif actualU2FChallengeCount != expectedU2FChallengeCount {\n\t\tt.Logf(\"REGRESSION BUG DETECTED:\")\n\t\tt.Logf(\"With %d U2F devices registered, the authentication
